## Section 001: Deep Exploration Lens Patterns
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 001 "Deep Exploration Lens Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that The seed title identifies a theme but never states when deep exploration is warranted, how its six workflow stages connect, or how a concise answer differs from an evidence-tested thesis.
- **supporting_reason:** Section 001 "Deep Exploration Lens Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because This sequence reduces the risk that a fluent first framing, fashionable option, or untested factual claim controls a consequential decision.
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 001 "Deep Exploration Lens Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: It becomes disproportionate for a narrow workable question that can be answered directly, and it becomes blocked when a material ambiguity or freshness-sensitive claim cannot be resolved within the permitted evidence boundary.
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 001 "Deep Exploration Lens Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: Assume analysis is requested, hidden chain-of-thought is excluded, and research permissions, source freshness, safety constraints, and user scope remain controlling.
- **revision_decision:** Section 001 "Deep Exploration Lens Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to Turn the title section into a use-or-compress decision and an explicit calibrate-premise-lens-map-evidence-challenge-verify-synthesize operating sequence.
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 001 "Deep Exploration Lens Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that Deep exploration is a correction architecture: each stage creates a different opportunity to invalidate framing, options, evidence, or confidence before the conclusion hardens.
### Question 02: What is the recommended default, and why?

## Section 002: Source Evidence Mapping Table
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 002 "Source Evidence Mapping Table", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that The seed lists three local files and three public URLs but does not explain the local files' complementary roles, their progressive loading order, or that the public pages were not retrieved in this no-browse pass.
- **supporting_reason:** Section 002 "Source Evidence Mapping Table", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because The local corpus explicitly prescribes progressive disclosure, while source presence alone neither proves relevance nor makes an external page current.
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 002 "Source Evidence Mapping Table", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: It fails when all six rows are treated as equal authority, all local files are loaded for every small task, or generic agent and CI documentation is cited as evidence for analytical quality.
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 002 "Source Evidence Mapping Table", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: No browsing occurred, public links cannot support present factual claims, and external conventions cannot override the local analytical workflow or the user's request.
- **revision_decision:** Section 002 "Source Evidence Mapping Table", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to Retain every source row while adding authority, progressive-loading, retrieval-state, claim-scope, and invalidation guidance.
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 002 "Source Evidence Mapping Table", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that Progressive source loading is epistemic control as well as context control: optional detail should enter only after the decision reveals which uncertainty it can reduce.

## Section 007: Anti Pattern Registry Table
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 007 "Anti Pattern Registry Table", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that The seed catches generic context-free, unsourced, and unverified guidance but omits the local corpus's central failures: premise laundering, theatrical lenses, decorative novelty, evidence conflation, fake challenge, hidden reasoning, and unverifiable certainty.
- **supporting_reason:** Section 007 "Anti Pattern Registry Table", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because Each failure creates the appearance of depth while removing a distinct correction mechanism from the workflow.
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 007 "Anti Pattern Registry Table", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: It fails when reviewers use labels without replaying the decision path, or when novelty and citation count are rewarded regardless of relevance.
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 007 "Anti Pattern Registry Table", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: Evaluate only explicit outputs and evidence, never demand private reasoning traces as proof of rigor.
- **revision_decision:** Section 007 "Anti Pattern Registry Table", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to Expand the registry from three generic failures to stage-specific premise, lens, option, evidence, challenge, verification, and synthesis failures.

## Section 008: Verification Gate Command Set
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 008 "Verification Gate Command Set", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that The seed supplies only a repository-wide archive command, which can validate generated structure but cannot verify a premise, lens relevance, evidence support, damaging counterexample, or thesis revision.
- **supporting_reason:** Section 008 "Verification Gate Command Set", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because Mechanical integrity and epistemic integrity are different claims, and the local verification pass explicitly requires evidence-driven revision rather than a ceremonial checklist.
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 008 "Verification Gate Command Set", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: It fails when a PASS is treated as truth, when verification questions merely restate claims, or when missing freshness-sensitive evidence is silently replaced by confidence.
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 008 "Verification Gate Command Set", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: The retained archive command proves only repository-level generation properties and must not be presented as domain validation.
- **revision_decision:** Section 008 "Verification Gate Command Set", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to Keep the command as one mechanical layer and add claim-level, adversarial, revision, and uncertainty gates.
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 008 "Verification Gate Command Set", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that Verification quality is measured by its power to change scope, confidence, or recommendation, not by the number of checks performed.

## Section 011: Decision Tradeoff Guide
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 011 "Decision Tradeoff Guide", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that The seed's Adopt, Adapt, Avoid, and Cost of being wrong rows describe generic source agreement but not the choice among full exploration, compressed analysis, premise-only correction, external research, direct answer, or scenario routing.
- **supporting_reason:** Section 011 "Decision Tradeoff Guide", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because Mode selection should scale correction effort to the expected cost of a wrong frame or unsupported conclusion.
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 011 "Decision Tradeoff Guide", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: It fails when full exploration becomes ceremony, compressed analysis skips a material falsifier, or direct response masks a disputed premise.
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 011 "Decision Tradeoff Guide", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: Mode choice cannot relax evidence honesty, hidden-reasoning guardrails, or user-imposed research limits.

- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 016 "Completeness Checklist", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: It fails as a memory list, when all checks are equally weighted, or when the artifact can pass without showing that challenge or verification affected the thesis.
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 016 "Completeness Checklist", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: Completeness means analysis-ready for delivery, not proof that uncertain empirical claims are true.

## Section 018: Workload Model
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 018 "Workload Model", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that The seed says one theme, all mapped sources, current external evidence, and one downstream review, which conflicts with progressive loading and omits the source-defined three-to-five lenses, three alternatives, and three-to-seven verified claims.
- **supporting_reason:** Section 018 "Workload Model", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because The source-defined ranges create useful breadth while one thesis owner protects convergence and avoids context growth for its own sake.
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 018 "Workload Model", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: It fails when multiple independent decisions, unbounded research, incompatible evidence standards, or several synthesis owners are forced into one brief.
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 018 "Workload Model", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: Parallel work must respect exclusive writes and cannot independently redefine the governing question or final thesis.
- **revision_decision:** Section 018 "Workload Model", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to Replace the all-sources heuristic with source-defined ranges, progressive loading, coupling limits, and one-owner synthesis.
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 018 "Workload Model", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that The scarce resource is not generation capacity but the integrator's ability to compare evidence under one stable premise.

## Section 021: Retry Backpressure Guidance
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that The seed offers one stale-evidence retry and generic checkpoint advice but does not distinguish retries for ambiguity, premise, lens selection, alternatives, evidence, challenge, or verification.
- **supporting_reason:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because Changed-condition retries preserve causal learning, whereas repeated broad exploration increases context, confidence, and narrative drift without resolving the blocker.
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: It is wrong when required research is prohibited, a user decision is missing, evidence is structurally unavailable, or the conclusion would trigger irreversible action under unresolved uncertainty.
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: Retries cannot bypass research prohibitions, fabricate missing evidence, expose hidden reasoning, or expand user-authorized scope.
- **revision_decision:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to Add stage-specific retry classes, one-condition changes, information-gain checks, and explicit stop or escalation paths.
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that Backpressure protects against epistemic sunk cost: effort already spent on a thesis is not evidence that another pass should preserve it.

## Section 023: Performance Verification Method

- **supporting_reason:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because A slower analysis can perform better when it prevents a costly wrong decision, while a fast literature dump can be operationally useless.
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: It fails on one-run percentiles, arbitrary ten-minute targets, lens or citation counts, or speed achieved by skipping challenge and verification.
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: Do not convert exploratory timing into an SLO or cross-domain benchmark without calibrated operational data.

## Section 024: Scale Boundary Statement
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that The seed names multiple systems, ownership boundaries, unbounded discovery, production traffic, context drift, and graph narrowing but does not explain how to split lenses, evidence, and theses without fragmenting the governing premise.
- **supporting_reason:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because Parallel work scales evidence collection, but only centralized convergence can reconcile incompatible definitions, confidence levels, and tradeoffs.
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: It fails when teams redefine the objective independently, share tightly coupled claims, race the canonical brief, or merge conclusions without cross-challenge.
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: Distributed execution must respect exclusive file ownership and cannot let a specialist silently expand scope or certainty.
- **revision_decision:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to Add evidence-domain decomposition, one-premise ownership, separate-decision briefs, merge gates, and no-split conditions.
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that Scale is reached when reconciliation cost and premise drift grow faster than the information gained from another parallel lens.
### Question 02: What is the recommended default, and why?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 02 on recommended default: the defensible default is to Split read-only evidence gathering by independent domain or lens, keep one owner for the premise and synthesis, use separate briefs for independent decisions, and integrate through a shared claim ledger, assumptions, and challenge pass.
- **supporting_reason:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 02 on recommended default: prefer that default because Parallel work scales evidence collection, but only centralized convergence can reconcile incompatible definitions, confidence levels, and tradeoffs.
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 02 on recommended default: do not present the default as universal; It fails when teams redefine the objective independently, share tightly coupled claims, race the canonical brief, or merge conclusions without cross-challenge.
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 02 on recommended default: the default assumes the following scope: Distributed execution must respect exclusive file ownership and cannot let a specialist silently expand scope or certainty.

- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 025 "Future Refresh Search Queries", Question 10 on second-order deductions: carry the deduction forward only within Future browsing requires authorization and cannot replace premise calibration or user-defined objectives.
- **revision_decision:** Section 025 "Future Refresh Search Queries", Question 10 on second-order deductions: change the guidance by applying this concrete revision: Retain the seed query categories only as labels and replace their text with claim-oriented templates and evidence-capture rules.
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 025 "Future Refresh Search Queries", Question 10 on second-order deductions: the resulting operational insight is to use Inspect provided sources, official tool help, local data, direct calculations, research papers, maintainers, or state an unresolved conditional conclusion. when the default cannot safely support how future authorized research should formulate queries that can confirm, falsify, or update a named claim

## Section 026: Evidence Boundary Notes
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 026 "Evidence Boundary Notes", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that The seed distinguishes local facts, external facts, and combined inference but omits user-supplied premises, verified versus unfetched external material, background knowledge, speculation, contradiction, confidence, and invalidation conditions.
- **supporting_reason:** Section 026 "Evidence Boundary Notes", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because Fine-grained boundaries prevent a plausible synthesis from laundering assumptions, stale memory, or public URL presence into evidence.
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 026 "Evidence Boundary Notes", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: It fails when one section label covers mixed claims, when inference language hides speculation, or when confidence is stated without describing contrary evidence.
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 026 "Evidence Boundary Notes", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: Expose explicit rationale and provenance without revealing hidden chain-of-thought or overstating unverified research.
- **revision_decision:** Section 026 "Evidence Boundary Notes", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to Extend the three seed labels into a claim-level evidence grammar with retrieval, contradiction, confidence, and invalidation metadata.
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 026 "Evidence Boundary Notes", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that Evidence boundaries make revision local: when one premise changes, reviewers can identify affected claims instead of discarding or preserving the entire thesis blindly.
